      googletag.display("home_fullpage0");

			var fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element = document.getElementById("home_fullpage0");
			// Set variable for initial refresh.
			var fullpage0_refreshed = false;

			if ( document.body.classList.contains("blog") && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
				// Go ahead and refresh on pages where it is visible.
				googletag.pubads().refresh([fullpagehome_fullpage0]);
				fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.classList.add("refreshed");

				// Refresh the ad only once.
				fullpage0_refreshed = true;

				// Remove the listener now.
				window.removeEventListener("scroll", fullpagehome_fullpage0_lazyListener);
			}

			// Add event listener for fullpage lazy loading.
			var fullpagehome_fullpage0_lazyListener = function() {

				// Value of scrollY at which the ad is about to come into view.
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
        var adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.offsetTop - (windowHeight * 1.5);
        
        var allowed = (fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.classList.contains("allowed") || 0 === 0) ? true : false;

				// Refresh the incontent slot when it is about to come into view.
				if ( window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue
        && ! fullpage0_refreshed
        && allowed
				&& window.innerWidth >= 925
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([fullpagehome_fullpage0]);
					fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.classList.add("refreshed");
					// console.log("home_fullpage initiated");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					fullpage0_refreshed = true;

					// Remove the listener now.
					window.removeEventListener("scroll", fullpagehome_fullpage0_lazyListener);
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(fullpagehome_fullpage0_lazyListener, 100));
			
			var fullpagehome_fullpage0_fired = 0;

			// Add event listener for fullpage active-view refresh.
			var fullpagehome_fullpage0_refreshListener = function() {

				var adHeight = fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.offsetHeight;
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adTop = fullpagehome_fullpage0_Element.offsetTop;
				var adVisibleScrollTop = adTop - windowHeight + ( adHeight * 0.7);
				var adVisibleScrollBottom = adTop + ( adHeight * 0.3);

				// console.log("adTop: " + adTop + ", window.scrollY: " + window.scrollY + ", adVisibleScrollTop: " + adVisibleScrollTop + ", adVisibleScrollBottom: " + adVisibleScrollBottom);

				if ( window.scrollY >= adVisibleScrollTop
				&& window.scrollY <= adVisibleScrollBottom
				&& fullpage0_refreshed
				&& 0 === fullpagehome_fullpage0_fired
				&& 0 !== adTop
				&& window.innerWidth >= 925
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") ) {
					// console.log("home_fullpage visible");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					fullpagehome_fullpage0_refreshInterval = setInterval( function() {
						googletag.pubads().refresh([fullpagehome_fullpage0]);
					}, 60000 );

					fullpagehome_fullpage0_fired = 1;

				} else if ( ( window.scrollY < adVisibleScrollTop || window.scrollY > adVisibleScrollBottom ) && 1 === fullpagehome_fullpage0_fired && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
					clearInterval(fullpagehome_fullpage0_refreshInterval);
					fullpagehome_fullpage0_fired = 0;
					// console.log("home_fullpage not visible");
				}
			}

       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         Product designer Ben Vessey developed 110 black and white, pixelated icons for today’s most popular apps, including Twitter, Tinder and Netflix. Dubbed the “iOS (Old School)” project, Vessey looked to Apple’s history to inform his clever designs. In addition to the app icons, Vessey created six monochromatic wallpapers. Together, the backgrounds and icons can be purchased for a little over $5 and installed on any …
        </p>

         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           In Paris’ 12th arrondissement, a new hotel-cinema hybrid called Hotel Paradiso (a reference to the 1966 film of the same name) welcomes guests to stay in one of 34 rooms or two suites, each of which doubles as a private screening room. Developed by movie theater group MK2 Nation, the hospitality venture includes room service, access to several streaming services and a selection of 2,500 …
          </p>

         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           Thirty minutes outside of Berlin, in an abandoned Bauhaus swimming pool from 1928 that sits across from E-WERK Luckenwalde renewable power station and contemporary arts center, the climate change opera Sun &amp; Sea will be staged 1-2 May. Created by three women artists in Lithuania—theater director Rugile Barzdziukaite, playwright Vaiva Grainyte and composer Lina Lapelyte—the opera won the 2019 Venice Biennale’s Golden Lion, after queues …
          </p>

             </a>
            </span>
           </p>

width="600"/>
         </a>
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           “In the internet era, true counterculture is difficult to see, and even harder to find—but that doesn’t mean it’s not there,” Berlin-based writer Caroline Busta writes in her Document Journal debut, “The internet didn’t kill counterculture—you just won’t find it on Instagram.” In her article, Busta points out that counterculture isn’t as simply classified as it used to be. Similarly, the powers that countercultures rebel …
          </p>
          <div class="entry-metadata">
           <p>
            <span class="source-link">
             Via
             <a href="https://www.documentjournal.com/2021/01/the-internet-didnt-kill-counterculture-you-just-wont-find-it-on-instagram/" target="_blank">
              documentjournal.com
             </a>
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>

              15 March 2021
             </time>
            </span>
           </p>
          </div>

         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           Digital artist Beeple (aka Mike Winkelmann) has sold his artwork “Everydays — The First 5000 Days”—a collage of the images that he posted daily since 2007—for a record setting $69.3 million. That’s a record (by far) for digital art and is the third highest auction price for a living artist in any medium. Following the sale of Chris Torres’s “Nyan Cat” work for $590,000 just …
          </p>
          <div class="entry-metadata">
           <p>
            <span class="source-link">
             Via
             <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/03/11/arts/design/nft-auction-christies-beeple.html" target="_blank">
              nytimes.com
             </a>
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
            <span class="posted-on">
             <span class="screen-reader-text">
              Posted on

             <time class="updated" datetime="2021-03-12T15:26:22-05:00">
              12 March 2021
             </time>
            </span>
           </p>

			googletag.display("home_incontent0");

			var currentAd = document.getElementById("home_incontent0");
			// Set variable for initial refresh.
			var incontent0_refreshed = false;

			if ( 0 === 0 && document.body.classList.contains("single") ) {
				currentAd.classList.add("allowed");

			if ( 0 === 0 && document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {
				googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent0]);
				currentAd.classList.add("refreshed");
				incontent0_refreshed = true;

				// Remove the listener now.
				window.removeEventListener("scroll", incontent0_lazyListener);

			if ( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {
				if ( 0 === 0 ) {
					var gridRowStart = (0 + 1) * 3;
					var gridRowEnd = gridRowStart + 1;
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowstart", gridRowStart);
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowend", gridRowEnd);

					var gridRowStart = ((0 + 1) * 5) - 2;

			var incontent0_lazyListener = function() {

				// Value of scrollY at which the ad is about to come into view.
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = currentAd.offsetTop - (windowHeight * 1.5);

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("post-type-archive-product") ) {
					var mainTop = document.getElementById("main").offsetTop;
					adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = adAlmostVisibleScrollValue + mainTop;
				}

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {

					// Find out how many products and ads are visible.
					var allProducts = document.getElementsByClassName("product");
					var visibleProducts = Array.prototype.filter.call(allProducts, function(product){
						return product.offsetHeight !== 0;
					});
					var numProductsVisible = visibleProducts.length;

					var numInContentAdsVisible = document.getElementsByClassName("incontent-ad refreshed").length;
					// console.log(numProductsVisible + ", " + numInContentAdsVisible);
					// console.log(numProductsVisible - ( 8 * numInContentAdsVisible ));

					var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 0;
					if ( 16 <= ( numProductsVisible - ( 16 * numInContentAdsVisible ) ) ) {
						var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 1;
					}
				}

				// Refresh the incontent slot when it is about to come into view.
				if ( ( window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue
				&& ! incontent0_refreshed
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("single") ||
				( document.body.classList.contains("single") && currentAd.classList.contains("allowed") ) )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") || 
				( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") && hasEnoughProductsVisible && 0 !== 0 ) ) ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent0]);
					currentAd.classList.add("refreshed");
					// console.log("incontent0 initiated");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					incontent0_refreshed = true;

					// Remove the listener now.
					window.removeEventListener("scroll", incontent0_lazyListener);
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent0_lazyListener, 100));
			
			var incontent0_fired = 0;

			// Add event listener for incontent active-view refresh.
			var incontent0_refreshListener = function() {

				if ( window.innerWidth < 925 ) {
					var headerHeight = document.getElementById("masthead").offsetHeight;
				} else {
					var headerHeight = 0;
				}

				var adHeight = currentAd.offsetHeight;
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adTop = currentAd.offsetTop;

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("post-type-archive-product") ) {
					var mainTop = document.getElementById("main").offsetTop;
					adTop = adTop + mainTop;
				}

				var adVisibleScrollTop = adTop - windowHeight + adHeight;
				var adVisibleScrollBottom = adTop - headerHeight;

				// console.log("window.scrollY: " + window.scrollY + ", adVisibleScrollTop: " + adVisibleScrollTop + ", adVisibleScrollBottom: " + adVisibleScrollBottom);

				if ( window.scrollY >= adVisibleScrollTop
				&& window.scrollY <= adVisibleScrollBottom
				&& incontent0_refreshed
				&& 0 === incontent0_fired
				&& 0 !== adTop
				&& 0 !== adHeight
				&& window.innerWidth >= 925
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") ) {
					// console.log("incontent0 visible");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					incontent0_refreshInterval = setInterval( function() {
						googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent0]);
					}, 60000 );

					incontent0_fired = 1;

				} else if ( ( window.scrollY < adVisibleScrollTop || window.scrollY > adVisibleScrollBottom ) && 1 === incontent0_fired && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
					clearInterval(incontent0_refreshInterval);
					incontent0_fired = 0;
					// console.log("incontent0 not visible");
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent0_refreshListener, 100));
		});

					var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 0;
					if ( 16 <= ( numProductsVisible - ( 16 * numInContentAdsVisible ) ) ) {
						var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 1;
					}
				}

				// Refresh the incontent slot when it is about to come into view.
				if ( ( window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue
				&& ! incontent1_refreshed
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("single") ||
				( document.body.classList.contains("single") && currentAd.classList.contains("allowed") ) )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") || 
				( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") && hasEnoughProductsVisible && 0 !== 1 ) ) ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent1]);
					currentAd.classList.add("refreshed");
					// console.log("incontent1 initiated");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					incontent1_refreshed = true;

					// Remove the listener now.
					window.removeEventListener("scroll", incontent1_lazyListener);
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent1_lazyListener, 100));
			
			var incontent1_fired = 0;

			// Add event listener for incontent active-view refresh.
			var incontent1_refreshListener = function() {

				if ( window.innerWidth < 925 ) {
					var headerHeight = document.getElementById("masthead").offsetHeight;
				} else {
					var headerHeight = 0;
				}

				var adHeight = currentAd.offsetHeight;
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adTop = currentAd.offsetTop;

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("post-type-archive-product") ) {
					var mainTop = document.getElementById("main").offsetTop;
					adTop = adTop + mainTop;
				}

				var adVisibleScrollTop = adTop - windowHeight + adHeight;
				var adVisibleScrollBottom = adTop - headerHeight;

				// console.log("window.scrollY: " + window.scrollY + ", adVisibleScrollTop: " + adVisibleScrollTop + ", adVisibleScrollBottom: " + adVisibleScrollBottom);

				if ( window.scrollY >= adVisibleScrollTop
				&& window.scrollY <= adVisibleScrollBottom
				&& incontent1_refreshed
				&& 0 === incontent1_fired
				&& 0 !== adTop
				&& 0 !== adHeight
				&& window.innerWidth >= 925
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") ) {
					// console.log("incontent1 visible");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					incontent1_refreshInterval = setInterval( function() {
						googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent1]);
					}, 60000 );

					incontent1_fired = 1;

				} else if ( ( window.scrollY < adVisibleScrollTop || window.scrollY > adVisibleScrollBottom ) && 1 === incontent1_fired && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
					clearInterval(incontent1_refreshInterval);
					incontent1_fired = 0;
					// console.log("incontent1 not visible");
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent1_refreshListener, 100));
		});
       </script>
      </div>
      <section class="two-column">

        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          From Stones Throw recording artist Sofie’s 2020 album Cult Survivor, “Happen 2 B There,” is transformed into a thumping dance tune by Frankfurt-based producer Lauer. The song’s underlying structure remains but Lauer’s emphasis on the instrumentation—digital drums, deep bass and robotic accents—amplifies the original.
         </p>

      <div class="incontent-ad google-ad" id="home_incontent2">
       <script>
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			var leaderMapping = googletag.sizeMapping().
	addSize([1375, 200], [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]]).
	addSize([1135, 200], [[728, 90]]).
	addSize([925, 200], [[300, 250]]).
	addSize([768, 200], [[728, 90]]).
	addSize([0, 0], [[300, 250], [320, 100], "fluid"]).
	build();
	
			var incontent2 = googletag.defineSlot("/1006677/home_incontent", [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90], [300, 250], [320, 100]], "home_incontent2").defineSizeMapping(leaderMapping).setTargeting("test","infinitescroll").addService(googletag.pubads());
			googletag.display("home_incontent2");

			var currentAd = document.getElementById("home_incontent2");
			// Set variable for initial refresh.
			var incontent2_refreshed = false;

			if ( 0 === 2 && document.body.classList.contains("single") ) {
				currentAd.classList.add("allowed");
			}

			if ( 0 === 2 && document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {
				googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent2]);
				currentAd.classList.add("refreshed");
				incontent2_refreshed = true;

				// Remove the listener now.
				window.removeEventListener("scroll", incontent2_lazyListener);
			}

			if ( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {
				if ( 0 === 2 ) {
					var gridRowStart = (2 + 1) * 3;
					var gridRowEnd = gridRowStart + 1;
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowstart", gridRowStart);
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowend", gridRowEnd);
				} else {
					var gridRowStart = ((2 + 1) * 5) - 2;
					var gridRowEnd = gridRowStart + 1;
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowstart", gridRowStart);
					currentAd.style.setProperty("--buyguideadgridrowend", gridRowEnd);
				}
			}

			// Add event listener for incontent lazy loading.
			var incontent2_lazyListener = function() {

				// Value of scrollY at which the ad is about to come into view.
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = currentAd.offsetTop - (windowHeight * 1.5);

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("post-type-archive-product") ) {
					var mainTop = document.getElementById("main").offsetTop;
					adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = adAlmostVisibleScrollValue + mainTop;
				}

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") ) {

					// Find out how many products and ads are visible.
					var allProducts = document.getElementsByClassName("product");
					var visibleProducts = Array.prototype.filter.call(allProducts, function(product){
						return product.offsetHeight !== 0;
					});
					var numProductsVisible = visibleProducts.length;

					var numInContentAdsVisible = document.getElementsByClassName("incontent-ad refreshed").length;
					// console.log(numProductsVisible + ", " + numInContentAdsVisible);
					// console.log(numProductsVisible - ( 8 * numInContentAdsVisible ));

					var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 0;
					if ( 16 <= ( numProductsVisible - ( 16 * numInContentAdsVisible ) ) ) {
						var hasEnoughProductsVisible = 1;
					}
				}

				// Refresh the incontent slot when it is about to come into view.
				if ( ( window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue
				&& ! incontent2_refreshed
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("single") ||
				( document.body.classList.contains("single") && currentAd.classList.contains("allowed") ) )
				&& ( ! document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") || 
				( document.body.classList.contains("coolhunting-productguide") && hasEnoughProductsVisible && 0 !== 2 ) ) ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent2]);
					currentAd.classList.add("refreshed");
					// console.log("incontent2 initiated");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					incontent2_refreshed = true;

					// Remove the listener now.
					window.removeEventListener("scroll", incontent2_lazyListener);
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent2_lazyListener, 100));
			
			var incontent2_fired = 0;

			// Add event listener for incontent active-view refresh.
			var incontent2_refreshListener = function() {

				if ( window.innerWidth < 925 ) {
					var headerHeight = document.getElementById("masthead").offsetHeight;
				} else {
					var headerHeight = 0;
				}

				var adHeight = currentAd.offsetHeight;
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adTop = currentAd.offsetTop;

				if ( document.body.classList.contains("post-type-archive-product") ) {
					var mainTop = document.getElementById("main").offsetTop;
					adTop = adTop + mainTop;
				}

				var adVisibleScrollTop = adTop - windowHeight + adHeight;
				var adVisibleScrollBottom = adTop - headerHeight;

				// console.log("window.scrollY: " + window.scrollY + ", adVisibleScrollTop: " + adVisibleScrollTop + ", adVisibleScrollBottom: " + adVisibleScrollBottom);

				if ( window.scrollY >= adVisibleScrollTop
				&& window.scrollY <= adVisibleScrollBottom
				&& incontent2_refreshed
				&& 0 === incontent2_fired
				&& 0 !== adTop
				&& 0 !== adHeight
				&& window.innerWidth >= 925
				&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") ) {
					// console.log("incontent2 visible");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					incontent2_refreshInterval = setInterval( function() {
						googletag.pubads().refresh([incontent2]);
					}, 60000 );

					incontent2_fired = 1;

				} else if ( ( window.scrollY < adVisibleScrollTop || window.scrollY > adVisibleScrollBottom ) && 1 === incontent2_fired && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
					clearInterval(incontent2_refreshInterval);
					incontent2_fired = 0;
					// console.log("incontent2 not visible");
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(incontent2_refreshListener, 100));
		});
       </script>

        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          Melbourne-based band Hiatus Kaiyote just signed to Flying Lotus-helmed label Brainfeeder, announced the new album Mood Valiant (set for release early this summer) and released their first new music since 2018, “Get Sun.” Featuring Brazilian composer/arranger Arthur Verocai, the song ebbs and flows with vibrancy; its last couple of minutes sprinkled with improv-sounding keys, ab-libs from front-woman Nai Palm, bird calls, fuzzy effects, glinting synths …
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          In advance of acclaimed French psych-rock act La Femme’s third LP, Paradigmes (out 2 April), the dazzling experimental rockers have released one more single “Le Sang de Mon Prochain.” Directed by Ilan Zerrouki, the mind-bending official music video pairs over-the-top costuming with theatrical performances. The retro-futuristic soundscape itself defies genre classification.
         </p>
        </div>

      <aside class="widget widget_googletag" id="fixed-nav-googletag">
       <!-- /1006677/home_nav -->
       <div class="googletag-widget google-ad" id="home_nav">
        <script>
         googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.display("home_nav");

			// Get the ad element.
			var fixedNavAd = document.getElementById("home_nav");

			// Refresh the fixed nav slot when it is about to come into view.
			var navRefreshed = false;

			if ( ! document.body.classList.contains("has-fullscreen-featured-post") && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {
				// Go ahead and refresh on pages where it is visible.
				googletag.pubads().refresh([fixed_nav]);

				navRefreshed = true;
				fixedNavAd.classList.add("refreshed");
			}	

			// Add scroll event listener for fixed nav lazy loading on desktop.
			var navLazyListener = function() {

				// Value of scrollY at which the ad is about to come into view.
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = fixedNavAd.offsetTop - (windowHeight * 1.5);

				if ( window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue && !navRefreshed && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([fixed_nav]);
					fixedNavAd.classList.add("refreshed");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					navRefreshed = true;
					// console.log("fixed_nav initiated");

					// Remove the listener now.
					window.removeEventListener("scroll", navLazyListener);
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("load", navLazyListener);
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(navLazyListener, 100));

			var navRefreshInterval = function() {
				// console.log("fixed_nav visible");
				googletag.pubads().refresh([fixed_nav]);
			};
			var navRefreshIntervalTime = 60000;

			// Add click event listener for fixed nav lazy loading on mobile.
			var sidebarToggle = document.getElementById("sidebar-toggle");
			var navLazyClickListener = function() {
				if ( !navRefreshed && window.innerWidth < 925 ) {

					// Refresh ad.
					googletag.pubads().refresh([fixed_nav]);
					fixedNavAd.classList.add("refreshed");

					// Refresh the ad only once.
					navRefreshed = true;
					// console.log("fixed_nav initiated mobile");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					// setInterval( navRefreshInterval, navRefreshIntervalTime );
					// navFired = 1;

				} else if ( navRefreshed && window.innerWidth < 925 && 0 === navFired ) {

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					// setInterval( navRefreshInterval, navRefreshIntervalTime );
					// navFired = 1;

				} else if ( navRefreshed && 1 === navFired ) {
					// clearInterval( navRefreshInterval );
					// navFired = 0;
					// console.log("fixed_nav not visible");
				}
			}
			sidebarToggle.addEventListener("click", navLazyClickListener);

			// Add event listener for fixed nav active-view refresh.
			var navFired = 0;
			var navRefreshListener = function() {

				var adHeight = fixedNavAd.offsetHeight;
				var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
				var adTop = fixedNavAd.offsetTop;
				var adVisibleScrollTop = adTop - windowHeight + adHeight;
				var adVisibleScrollBottom = adTop;

				if ( ( ( window.innerWidth >= 925 && window.scrollY >= adVisibleScrollTop && window.scrollY <= adVisibleScrollBottom )
					|| ( window.innerWidth >= 925 && document.body.classList.contains("fixed") ) )
					&& navRefreshed
					&& 0 === navFired ) {

					// console.log("fixed_nav visible");

					// Set timer to refresh slot every 60 seconds
					setInterval( navRefreshInterval, navRefreshIntervalTime );

					navFired = 1;
				} else if ( ( ( window.scrollY < adVisibleScrollTop || window.scrollY > adVisibleScrollBottom )
					&& ! document.body.classList.contains("fixed")
					&& ! document.body.classList.contains("sidebar-open") )
					&& 1 === navFired && window.innerWidth >= 925 ) {

					clearInterval( navRefreshInterval );
					navFired = 0;
					// console.log("fixed_nav not visible");
				}
			}
			window.addEventListener("scroll", _.throttle(navRefreshListener, 100));
		});
        </script>
       </div>
